Definition right_lifting_data (J : morphism_class C) (f : arrow C) : UU :=
    ∏ (g : arrow C), (J _ _ g) -> elp g f.


C: category
J: morphism_class C
f, f': arrow C

right_lifting_data J f → right_lifting_data J f'

(* filler lifting problem g --> f commutes with mn and the filler of
   g --> f --> f' in the right way *)
Definition right_lifting_data_comp {J : morphism_class C} {f f' : arrow C}
    (δ : right_lifting_data J f) (δ' : right_lifting_data J f') (mn : f --> f') : UU :=
  ∏ (g : arrow C) (H : J _ _ g) (S : g --> f),
  (filler_map (δ g H _ _ (arrow_mor_comm S))) · (arrow_mor00 mn) =
    filler_map (δ' g H _ _ (arrow_mor_comm (S · mn))).


C: category
J: morphism_class C
f, f': arrow C
δ: right_lifting_data J f
δ': right_lifting_data J f'
mn: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
isaprop (right_lifting_data_comp δ δ' mn)


C: category
J: morphism_class C
f, f': arrow C
δ: right_lifting_data J f
δ': right_lifting_data J f'
mn: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
isaprop (right_lifting_data_comp δ δ' mn)

  
C: category
J: morphism_class C
f, f': arrow C
δ: right_lifting_data J f
δ': right_lifting_data J f'
mn: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
t: arrow C
t0: J (pr11 t) (pr21 t) (pr2 t)
t1: arrow C ⟦ t, f ⟧
isofhlevel 1
  (filler_map
     (δ t t0 (pr11 t1) (pr21 t1) (arrow_mor_comm t1))
   · arrow_mor00 mn =
   filler_map
     (δ' t t0 (pr11 (t1 · mn)) (pr21 (t1 · mn))
        (arrow_mor_comm (t1 · mn))))

  apply homset_property.
Qed.

    (* commutativity of lifting data:
       solution of lifting problem S must commute with mn: g --> g':
                   m
       a ----> x ----> x'

       v       v       v
       b ----> y ----> y'
                   n
      δ : b --> x
      δ': b --> x'

Definition rlp_morcls (J : morphism_class C) : category :=
    total_category (rlp_morcls_disp J).

(* needed later *)
(* all lifting problems of J wrt. g *)
Definition morcls_lp (J : morphism_class C) (f : arrow C) : UU :=
    ∑ (g : total_category (morcls_disp J)), (pr1 g) --> f.

Coercion morcls_lp_diagram {J : morphism_class C} {f : arrow C} (lp : morcls_lp J f) := pr2 lp.
Definition morcls_lp_map {J : morphism_class C} {f : arrow C} (lp : morcls_lp J f) := pr1 lp.

  disp_functor (functor_identity _) (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n).

η: disp_functor (functor_identity (arrow C))
  (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n)
f, f': arrow C
ff: nwfs_R_maps n f
ff': nwfs_R_maps n f'
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: ff -->[ S] ff'
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
pr1 (R_map_section (η g Jg))
· (three_mor11
     ((# n)%cat
        (mors_to_arrow_mor (pr2 g) (pr2 f) (pr11 Sgf)
           (pr21 Sgf) (arrow_mor_comm Sgf)))
   · (pr1 (L_map_retraction ff) · arrow_mor00 S)) =
filler_map
  (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_on_objects η f' ff' g Jg
     (pr11 (Sgf · S)) (pr21 (Sgf · S))
     (arrow_mor_comm (Sgf · S)))

C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: disp_functor (functor_identity (arrow C))
  (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n)
f, f': arrow C
αf: arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f, f ⟧
αflaws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f αf)
ff': nwfs_R_maps n f'
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: (αf,, αflaws) -->[ S] ff'
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
pr1 (section_disp_on_morphisms (pr1 n) S)
· pr1 (L_map_retraction ff') =
pr1 (L_map_retraction (αf,, αflaws)) · arrow_mor00 S

  
C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: disp_functor (functor_identity (arrow C))
  (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n)
f, f': arrow C
αf: arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f, f ⟧
αflaws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f αf)
αf': arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f', f' ⟧
αf'laws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f' αf')
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: (αf,, αflaws) -->[ S] (αf',, αf'laws)
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
pr1 (section_disp_on_morphisms (pr1 n) S)
· pr1 (L_map_retraction (αf',, αf'laws)) =
pr1 (L_map_retraction (αf,, αflaws)) · arrow_mor00 S

  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f' αf')
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: (αf,, αflaws) -->[ S] (αf',, αf'laws)
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
S11:= three_mor11 ((# n)%cat S): C ⟦ pr12 (n f), pr12 (n f') ⟧
pr1 (section_disp_on_morphisms (pr1 n) S)
· pr1 (L_map_retraction (αf',, αf'laws)) =
pr1 (L_map_retraction (αf,, αflaws)) · arrow_mor00 S

  
C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: disp_functor (functor_identity (arrow C))
  (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n)
f, f': arrow C
αf: arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f, f ⟧
αflaws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f αf)
αf': arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f', f' ⟧
αf'laws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f' αf')
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: (αf,, αflaws) -->[ S] (αf',, αf'laws)
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
S11:= three_mor11 ((# n)%cat S): C ⟦ pr12 (n f), pr12 (n f') ⟧
S11 · arrow_mor00 αf' = arrow_mor00 αf · arrow_mor00 S


  (*         S00
      ++++> +++++>
    |      |      |
    |   λf |      |λf'
    |      v S11  v
 ρf | αf    +++++> +++++++>
    |      |      |        |
    |   ρf |      |ρf' αf' | f'
    v      v      v        v
      ===== -----> ========
            S22
  Need to show that the +++> maps are equal
  This follows from the fact that S is an algebra map (Sisalg)
  *)

  (* simpl in Sisalg. *)
  (* unfold is_Algebra_mor in Sisalg. *)
  
C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: disp_functor (functor_identity (arrow C))
  (morcls_disp J) (nwfs_L_maps n)
f, f': arrow C
αf: arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f, f ⟧
αflaws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f αf)
αf': arrow C ⟦ nwfs_R_monad n f', f' ⟧
αf'laws: Algebra_laws (nwfs_R_monad n)
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
     (nwfs_R_monad n) f' αf')
S: arrow C ⟦ f, f' ⟧
Sisalg: (αf,, αflaws) -->[ S] (αf',, αf'laws)
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
Sgf: arrow C ⟦ g, functor_identity (arrow C) f ⟧
S11:= three_mor11 ((# n)%cat S): C ⟦ pr12 (n f), pr12 (n f') ⟧
top_line:= arrow_mor00_eq Sisalg: arrow_mor00
  (Alg_map (nwfs_R_monad n)
     (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
        (nwfs_R_monad n) f
        (pr1 (αf,, αflaws)),,
      pr2 (αf,, αflaws)
      :
      Algebra (nwfs_R_monad n)) · S) =
arrow_mor00
  ((# (nwfs_R_monad n))%cat S
   · Alg_map (nwfs_R_monad n)
       (MonadAlgebras.make_Algebra_data
          (nwfs_R_monad n) f'
          (pr1 (αf',, αf'laws)),,
        pr2 (αf',, αf'laws)
        :
        Algebra (nwfs_R_monad n)))
S11 · arrow_mor00 αf' = arrow_mor00 αf · arrow_mor00 S

  (* simpl in top_line. *)
  exact (pathsinv0 top_line).
Qed.


(* "this assignation extends to a functor θ: R-Map ⟶ J□", Garner 2007, p18 *)
Definition R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data (η : morcls_L_map_structure J) :
    disp_functor_data (functor_identity _) (nwfs_R_maps n) (rlp_morcls_disp J) :=
  (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_on_objects η,, R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_on_displayed_mors η).


C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: morcls_L_map_structure J
disp_functor_axioms
  (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η)


C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: morcls_L_map_structure J
disp_functor_axioms
  (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η)

  
C: category
n: nwfs C
J: morphism_class C
η: morcls_L_map_structure J
(∏ (x : arrow C) (xx : nwfs_R_maps n x),
 ♯ (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η) (id_disp xx) =
 transportb
   (mor_disp (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η x xx)
      (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η x xx))
   (functor_id (functor_identity (arrow C)) x)
   (id_disp (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η x xx)))
× (∏ (x y z : arrow C) (xx : nwfs_R_maps n x)
   (yy : pr1 (nwfs_R_maps n) y)
   (zz : pr1 (nwfs_R_maps n) z) (f : arrow C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
   (g : arrow C ⟦ y, z ⟧) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
   (gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
   ♯ (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η) (ff ;; gg) =
   transportb
     (mor_disp
        (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η x xx)
        (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η z zz))
     (functor_comp (functor_identity (arrow C)) f g)
     (♯ (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η) ff ;; 
      ♯ (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_data η) gg))

  split; intros; apply isaprop_lifting_data_comp.
Qed.

Definition R_map_rlp_morcls_structure (η : morcls_L_map_structure J) :
    disp_functor (functor_identity _) (nwfs_R_maps n) (rlp_morcls_disp J) :=
  (_,, R_map_rlp_morcls_structure_axioms η).

(* Garner 2008, Definition 3.9 / Garner 2007, p18*)
(* we say that n := (L, R, Δ) is cofibrantly generated by (J, η) if θ is
   an isomorphism of categories *)
Definition cofibrantly_generated (η : morcls_L_map_structure J) :=
    is_equiv_over (_,, identity_functor_is_adj_equivalence) (R_map_rlp_morcls_structure η).

Definition algebraically_free : UU :=
    ∑ η : morcls_L_map_structure J, cofibrantly_generated η.

   ∥ rlp_morcls_disp J f ∥)

           (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,
            CoequalizerArrow C coeq), w ⟧,
 pr2
   (CoequalizerObject C coeq,, CoequalizerArrow C coeq)
 · t = h) y → y = ?x

      
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
H, z: C
g, f': C ⟦ H, z ⟧
coeq:= CCoequalizers H z g f': Coequalizer C g f'
w: C
h: C ⟦ z, w ⟧
Hw: g · h = f' · h
C
⟦ pr1
    (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,
     CoequalizerArrow C coeq), w ⟧
 exact (CoequalizerOut _ coeq _ h Hw).

∏

  ((λ t : C

       ⟦ pr1
           (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,

C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
H, z: C
g, f': C ⟦ H, z ⟧
coeq:= CCoequalizers H z g f': Coequalizer C g f'
w: C
h: C ⟦ z, w ⟧
Hw: g · h = f' · h
y: C
⟦ pr1
    (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,
     CoequalizerArrow C coeq), w ⟧
Hy: (λ t : C
       ⟦ pr1
           (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,
            CoequalizerArrow C coeq), w ⟧,
 pr2
   (CoequalizerObject C coeq,,
    CoequalizerArrow C coeq) · t = h) y
y = CoequalizerOut C coeq w h Hw

        exact (CoequalizerOutUnique _ _ _ _ _ _ Hy).
Qed.

Definition morcls_lp_dom_coprod :=
  CC (λ (g : morcls_lp J f), arrow_dom (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))).
Definition morcls_lp_cod_coprod :=
  CC (λ (g : morcls_lp J f), arrow_cod (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))).

Definition morcls_lp_coprod :=
 (CoproductOfArrows' _ _
   morcls_lp_dom_coprod morcls_lp_cod_coprod
   (λ (S : morcls_lp J f), arrow_mor (pr1 (morcls_lp_map S)))).

(* the canonical diagram capturing all lifting problems in J *)

HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
arrow C ⟦ morcls_lp_coprod, f ⟧

C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
CoproductArrow morcls_lp_dom_coprod
  (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor00 j) · pr2 f =
morcls_lp_coprod
· CoproductArrow morcls_lp_cod_coprod
    (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor11 j)
 abstract (
      etrans; [apply postcompWithCoproductArrow|];
      apply pathsinv0;
      etrans; [apply precompWithCoproductArrow|];
      apply pathsinv0;
      apply maponpaths;
      apply funextsec;
      intro j;
      exact (arrow_mor_comm j)
    ).
Defined.

(* It is possible to show this more generally for _any_
   coproduct of maps in J, but this is not really necessary or useful
   for us.

   The proof of this lemma is practically the same as that of
   wfs_closed_coproducts, but we do _not_ need the axiom of choice here,
   since we know the actual lifting data. *)

C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_dom (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) j, pr11 f ⟧
kj:= λ j : morcls_lp J f,
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · k: ∏ j : morcls_lp J f,
C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_cod (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) j, pr21 f ⟧
jlift: ∏ j : morcls_lp J f,
∑ lj : C ⟦ pr211 (pr1 j), pr11 f ⟧,
pr211 j · lj = hj j × lj · pr2 f = kj j
lj: ∏ x : morcls_lp J f, C ⟦ pr211 (pr1 x), pr11 f ⟧
hlj: ∏ x : morcls_lp J f,
pr211 x · lj x = hj x × lj x · pr2 f = kj x
l: C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f ⟧
hl: ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i · l = lj i
uniqueness: ∏
t : ∑
    g : C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f
        ⟧,
    ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
    CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i
    · g = lj i, t = l,, hl
morcls_lp_coprod
· CoproductArrow morcls_lp_cod_coprod
    (λ i : morcls_lp J f,
     CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i · l) =
CoproductArrow morcls_lp_dom_coprod
  (λ i : morcls_lp J f,
   CoproductIn morcls_lp_dom_coprod i · h)

∑ lj : C ⟦ pr211 (pr1 j), pr11 f ⟧,

uniqueness: ∏

        ⟧,

j: morcls_lp J f

pr1 (morcls_lp_map j)
· (CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · l)

    g : C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f
        ⟧,
    ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
    CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i
    · g = lj i, t = l,, hl
j: morcls_lp J f
kljcomm: lj j · pr2 f = kj j
lj j = ?f'
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
rldJf: right_lifting_data J f
h: C ⟦ morcls_lp_dom_coprod, pr11 f ⟧
k: C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr21 f ⟧
S: h · pr2 f = morcls_lp_coprod · k
hj:= λ j : morcls_lp J f,
CoproductIn morcls_lp_dom_coprod j · h: ∏ j : morcls_lp J f,
C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_dom (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) j, pr11 f ⟧
kj:= λ j : morcls_lp J f,
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · k: ∏ j : morcls_lp J f,
C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_cod (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) j, pr21 f ⟧
jlift: ∏ j : morcls_lp J f,
∑ lj : C ⟦ pr211 (pr1 j), pr11 f ⟧,
pr211 j · lj = hj j × lj · pr2 f = kj j
lj: ∏ x : morcls_lp J f, C ⟦ pr211 (pr1 x), pr11 f ⟧
hlj: ∏ x : morcls_lp J f,
pr211 x · lj x = hj x × lj x · pr2 f = kj x
l: C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f ⟧
hl: ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i · l = lj i
uniqueness: ∏
t : ∑
    g : C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f
        ⟧,
    ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
    CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i
    · g = lj i, t = l,, hl
j: morcls_lp J f
kljcomm: lj j · pr2 f = kj j
?f' · pr2 f =
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · l · pr2 f

            
C: category

f: arrow C
rldJf: right_lifting_data J f

    g : C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f
        ⟧,
    ∏ i : morcls_lp J f,
    CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod i
    · g = lj i, t = l,, hl
j: morcls_lp J f
kljcomm: lj j · pr2 f = kj j
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · l · pr2 f =
CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod j · l · pr2 f

    reflexivity.
Qed.

morcls_lp_dom_coprod ⟧

domg_in · arrow_mor00 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram

?b = domg_in · arrow_mor00 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram

  (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor11 j)

Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
h: C ⟦ pr11 g, pr11 f ⟧
k: C ⟦ pr21 g, pr21 f ⟧
H: h · pr2 f = pr2 g · k
Jtot:= total_category (morcls_disp J): category
g':= g,, Jg : Jtot: Jtot
Hlp:= g',, make_dirprod h k,, H : morcls_lp J f: morcls_lp J f
codg_in:= CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod Hlp: C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_cod (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) Hlp,
morcls_lp_cod_coprod ⟧
domg_in:= CoproductIn morcls_lp_dom_coprod Hlp: C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_dom (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) Hlp,
morcls_lp_dom_coprod ⟧
k =
codg_in
· CoproductArrow morcls_lp_cod_coprod
    (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor11 j)


    (* k = codf_in · kj *)
    (* unfold codf_in. *)
    
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
ltot: C ⟦ morcls_lp_cod_coprod, pr11 f ⟧
Hl1: morcls_lp_coprod · ltot =
CoproductArrow morcls_lp_dom_coprod
  (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor00 j)
Hl2: ltot · pr2 f =
CoproductArrow morcls_lp_cod_coprod
  (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor11 j)
g: arrow C
Jg: J (pr11 g) (pr21 g) (pr2 g)
h: C ⟦ pr11 g, pr11 f ⟧
k: C ⟦ pr21 g, pr21 f ⟧
H: h · pr2 f = pr2 g · k
Jtot:= total_category (morcls_disp J): category
g':= g,, Jg : Jtot: Jtot
Hlp:= g',, make_dirprod h k,, H : morcls_lp J f: morcls_lp J f
codg_in:= CoproductIn morcls_lp_cod_coprod Hlp: C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_cod (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) Hlp,
morcls_lp_cod_coprod ⟧
domg_in:= CoproductIn morcls_lp_dom_coprod Hlp: C
⟦ (λ g : morcls_lp J f,
   arrow_dom (pr1 (morcls_lp_map g))) Hlp,
morcls_lp_dom_coprod ⟧
codg_in
· CoproductArrow morcls_lp_cod_coprod
    (λ j : morcls_lp J f, arrow_mor11 j) = k

    exact (CoproductInCommutes (morcls_lp_cod_coprod) _ Hlp).
Qed.

(*
We turn the diagram
          h_x
    ∑A_x ----> C
     |         |
∑f_x |         | g
     v         v
    ∑B_x ----> D
          k_x

into the pushout diagram
         h_x
    ∑A_x ----> C--\
     |         |  |
∑f_x |     λ1g |  \
     v         v   |
    ∑B_x ---> E1g  | id · g
      \__       \  |
         \_   ρ1g|
      k_x  \_____ \|
                   D
using the pushout property. Inserting an identity morphism gives a diagram
          h_x
    ∑A_x ----> C ====== C
     |         |        |
∑f_x |         | λ1g    |
     v         v        v
    ∑B_x ---> E1g ----> D  ~~> k_x
                   ρ1g
*)

Definition morcls_lp_coprod_diagram_pushout :
    Pushout (morcls_lp_coprod) (arrow_mor00 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram) :=
  POs _ _ _ (morcls_lp_coprod) (arrow_mor00 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram).

Definition E1 : C :=
  PushoutObject morcls_lp_coprod_diagram_pushout.
Definition λ1 : (arrow_dom f) --> E1 :=
  PushoutIn2 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram_pushout.
Definition ρ1 : E1 --> (arrow_cod f) :=
  PushoutArrow
    morcls_lp_coprod_diagram_pushout
    _ (arrow_mor11 morcls_lp_coprod_diagram)
    f (pathsinv0 (arrow_mor_comm morcls_lp_coprod_diagram)).


C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
λ1 · ρ1 = pr2 f


C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
λ1 · ρ1 = pr2 f

  
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
λ1 · ρ1 = ?b
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
?b = pr2 f
 
C: category
HCC: Colims C
J: morphism_class C
f: arrow C
pr2 f = pr2 f

  reflexivity.
Qed.
